tools/list

client„ĀĮserver„ĀĆŚÖ¨ťĖč„Āô„āčtool„āíŚŹĖŚĺó„Āô„āč„Äā„Āď„Āď„ĀßŤŅĒ„āčname„ÄĀdescription„ÄĀinputSchema„ÄĀŚŅÖŤ¶Ā„Ā™„āČoutputSchema„ĀĆ„ÄĀhostŚĀī„ĀßLLM„Āęśł°„Āē„āĆ„āčtoolŚģöÁĺ©„ĀģśĚźśĖô„Āę„Ā™„āč„Äā

  "method": "tools/list",
  "params": {}
}
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": 2,
  "result": {
    "tools": [
      {
        "name": "inventory.search_items",
        "title": "Search inventory items",
        "description": "Search inventory items by keyword. Use this before reserving stock when the exact SKU is unknown. Returns at most 20 items with stable item IDs.",
        "inputSchema": {
          "type": "object",
          "properties": {
            "query": {
              "type": "string",
              "description": "Keyword, product name, or SKU fragment."
            },
            "limit": {
              "type": "integer",
              "minimum": 1,
              "maximum": 20,
              "default": 10
            }
          },
          "required": ["query"],
          "additionalProperties": false
        },
        "outputSchema": {
          "type": "object",
          "properties": {
            "items": {
              "type": "array",
              "items": {
                "type": "object",
                "properties": {
                  "item_id": { "type": "string" },
                  "name": { "type": "string" },
                  "stock": { "type": "integer" }
                },
                "required": ["item_id", "name", "stock"]
              }
            }
          },
          "required": ["items"]
        }
      }
    ]
  }
}

MCP serverśßčÁĮČ: engineerŚźĎ„ĀĎpattern

Á§ĺŚÜÖŚźĎ„ĀĎ„ĀęśúČÁĒ®„Ā™„Āģ„ĀĮ„ÄĆMCP„Ā®„ĀĮšĹē„Āč„Äć„Ā†„ĀĎ„Āß„ĀĮ„Ā™„ĀŹ„ÄĀ„ÄĆśóĘŚ≠ė„ā∑„āĻ„ÉÜ„É†„āímodel„ĀĆšĹŅ„Āą„āčtool„Ā®„Āó„Ā¶ŚģČŚÖ®„ĀęŚÖ¨ťĖč„Āô„āč„Āę„ĀĮ„Ā©„ĀÜ„Āô„āč„Āč„Äć„ÄāŚģüÁĒ®šłä„ĀĮ3„Ā§„Āģpattern„ĀĆ„Āā„āč„Äā

  1. šĺ°ŚÄ§„Āģťęė„ĀĄŚįĎśēįoperation„āíšł≠ŚŅÉ„Āę„ÄĀŚįŹ„Āē„Ā™MCP server„āíśČčśõł„Āć„Āô„āč„Äā
  2. śóĘŚ≠ėOpenAPI spec„Āč„āČMCP surface„āíÁĒüśąź„Āó„ÄĀ„ĀĚ„ĀģŚĺĆfilter/hardening„Āô„āč„Äā
  3. HTTPSšłä„ĀģRemote MCP server„Ā®„Āó„Ā¶deploy„Āó„ÄĀClaude„ÄĀClaude Code„ÄĀ„ĀĚ„ĀģšĽĖMCP client„Āč„āČśé•Á∂ö„Āß„Āć„āč„āą„ĀÜ„Āę„Āô„āč„Äā

Pattern A: FastMCP„Āßtool„āíśČčśõł„Āć„Āô„āč

„Āď„āĆ„ĀĮŚįŹ„Āē„ĀŹcurated„Āē„āĆ„Āütool surface„ĀęŚźĎ„ĀŹ„ÄāŚěčhint„Ā®docstring„ĀĆ„ÄĀmodel„Āč„āČŤ¶č„Āą„āčschema„Ā®description„Āę„Ā™„āč„Äā

from mcp.server.fastmcp import FastMCP

mcp = FastMCP("inventory")

@mcp.tool()
async def get_stock(item_id: str) -> dict:
    """Return current inventory stock for one item."""
    # Replace with DB/API call.
    return {"item_id": item_id, "stock": 42}

@mcp.tool()
async def reserve_stock(item_id: str, quantity: int) -> dict:
    """Reserve inventory for an order. Use only after user confirmation."""
    if quantity <= 0:
        raise ValueError("quantity must be positive")
    return {"item_id": item_id, "reserved": quantity}

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Local MCP for desktop clients.
    mcp.run(transport="stdio")

stdio server„Āß„ĀĮ„ÄĀstdout„ĀĆprotocol channel„Ā™„Āģ„ĀßťÄöŚłłlog„āístdout„ĀłŚáļ„Āó„Ā¶„ĀĮ„ĀĄ„ĀĎ„Ā™„ĀĄ„Äāstderr„Āčstructured logging„āíšĹŅ„ĀÜ„Äā

Pattern B: śóĘŚ≠ėFastAPI + OpenAPI„āíMCPŚĆĖ„Āô„āč

FastAPI„ĀĮ/openapi.json„ĀßOpenAPI„āíŤá™ŚčēŚÖ¨ťĖč„Āó„ÄĀapp.openapi()„Āß„āāŚźĆ„Āėschema„āíprocessŚÜÖ„ĀßŚŹĖŚĺó„Āß„Āć„āč„Äā„ĀĚ„Āģ„Āü„āĀ„ÄĀFastAPI„ĀĮMCP wrapper„ĀģŚÖÉ„Āę„Āó„āĄ„Āô„ĀĄ„Äā

śóĘŚ≠ėAPI:

# inventory_api.py
from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException
from pydantic import BaseModel

app = FastAPI(title="Inventory API", version="1.0.0")

class Item(BaseModel):
    id: str
    name: str
    stock: int

ITEMS = {
    "sku-001": Item(id="sku-001", name="Notebook", stock=42),
}

@app.get("/items/{item_id}", tags=["items"])
async def get_item(item_id: str) -> Item:
    """Get a single item by SKU."""
    item = ITEMS.get(item_id)
    if item is None:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="item not found")
    return item

@app.post("/items/{item_id}/reserve", tags=["inventory"])
async def reserve_item(item_id: str, quantity: int) -> dict[str, int]:
    """Reserve stock for an item."""
    item = ITEMS.get(item_id)
    if item is None:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="item not found")
    if quantity <= 0 or quantity > item.stock:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="invalid quantity")
    item.stock -= quantity
    return {"reserved": quantity, "remaining": item.stock}

OpenAPI schema„Āč„āČšĹú„āčMCP wrapper:

# inventory_mcp.py
import httpx
from fastmcp import FastMCP
from inventory_api import app

openapi_spec = app.openapi()
api_client = httpx.AsyncClient(base_url="http://127.0.0.1:9000")

mcp = FastMCP.from_openapi(
    openapi_spec=openapi_spec,
    client=api_client,
    name="Inventory MCP",
)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Remote-capable HTTP transport. Put HTTPS/auth in front for production.
    mcp.run(transport="http", host="0.0.0.0", port=8000)

localŚģüŤ°Ć:

uvicorn inventory_api:app --host 127.0.0.1 --port 9000
python inventory_mcp.py

OpenAPIÁĒüśąź„ĀĮŚáļÁôļÁāĻ„Āę„Āô„Āé„Ā™„ĀĄ„Äāproduction MCP server„Āß„ĀĮ„ÄĀ„Āô„ĀĻ„Ā¶„Āģendpoint„āíÁĄ°Ś∑ģŚą•„ĀęŚÖ¨ťĖč„Āó„Ā¶„ĀĮ„ĀĄ„ĀĎ„Ā™„ĀĄ„Äāmodel-facing tool surface„āícurate„Āô„āčŚŅÖŤ¶Ā„ĀĆ„Āā„āč„Äā

Pattern C: ÁĒüśąź„Āē„āĆ„Āütool„āíŚÖ¨ťĖčŚČć„Āęfilter„Āô„āč

route mapping„āíšĹŅ„ĀĄ„ÄĀinternal„Āĺ„Āü„ĀĮdangerous„Ā™endpoint„āíťô§Ś§Ė„Āó„ÄĀŚźĄroute„āítool/resource/resource template„Āģ„Ā©„āĆ„Ā®„Āó„Ā¶ŚÖ¨ťĖč„Āô„āč„Āč„āíśĪļ„āĀ„āč„Äā

from fastmcp import FastMCP
from fastmcp.server.providers.openapi import MCPType
from fastmcp.utilities.openapi import HTTPRoute

def route_map_fn(route: HTTPRoute, mcp_type: MCPType) -> MCPType | None:
    if route.path.startswith("/admin/"):
        return MCPType.EXCLUDE
    if "internal" in set(route.tags or []):
        return MCPType.EXCLUDE
    if route.method in {"POST", "PUT", "PATCH", "DELETE"}:
        return MCPType.TOOL
    if route.path.startswith("/items/"):
        return MCPType.RESOURCE_TEMPLATE
    return None

mcp = FastMCP.from_openapi(
    openapi_spec=openapi_spec,
    client=api_client,
    name="Inventory MCP",
    route_map_fn=route_map_fn,
)

internal API„Āß„ĀĮ„ÄĀ„Āď„Āģfiltering layer„Āęengineering judgment„ĀĆśúÄ„āāŤ°®„āĆ„āč„Äā

  • AI assistant„ĀĆŚģüťöõ„ĀęŚĎľ„Ā∂„ĀĻ„Āćoperation„Ā†„ĀĎ„āíśģč„Āô„Äā
  • „Āĺ„Āöread-only tool„āíŚĄ™ŚÖą„Āó„ÄĀwrite tool„ĀĮconfirmation„Ā®authorization„ĀģŚĺĆ„āć„ĀęÁĹģ„ĀŹ„Äā
  • „Āô„ĀĻ„Ā¶„Āģoperation„ĀęŚģČŚģö„Āó„ĀüoperationId„ÄĀśėéÁĘļ„Ā™tag„ÄĀś≠£ÁĘļ„Ā™request/response schema„ÄĀÁį°śĹĒ„Ā™description„āíšĽė„ĀĎ„āč„Äā
  • side effect„ĀĆśõĖśėß„Ā™endpoint„āíŚÖ¨ťĖč„Āó„Ā™„ĀĄ„Äā
  • pagination„Ā®output cap„āíŚÖ•„āĆ„āč„ÄāŚ∑®Ś§ß„Ā™ÁĒüAPI response„ĀĮmodel context„Ā®„Āó„Ā¶Ť≥™„ĀĆšĹé„ĀĄ„Äā

engineerŚźĎ„ĀĎMCP serverŤ®≠Ť®ą„Éę„Éľ„Éę

ťáćŤ¶Ā„Ā™Ť®≠Ť®ą„Éę„Éľ„Éę:

  • Tool surface„ĀĮŚćė„Ā™„āčAPI wrapping„Āß„ĀĮ„Ā™„ĀŹproduct design„Äāmodel„ĀĮname„ÄĀdescription„ÄĀparameter„ÄĀresult„āíŤ¶č„āč„Āü„āĀ„ÄĀśĄŹŚõ≥„Āó„Ā¶Ť®≠Ť®ą„Āô„āč„Äā
  • OpenAPI quality„ĀĮMCP quality„āíÁõīśé•śĪļ„āĀ„āč„Äāśā™„ĀĄoperationId„ÄĀŚľĪ„ĀĄschema„ÄĀśõĖśėß„Ā™description„ÄĀŚ∑®Ś§ß„Ā™response body„ĀĮśā™„ĀĄtool„Āę„Ā™„āč„Äā
  • read-only„Āč„āČŚßč„āĀ„ÄĀ„ĀĚ„ĀģŚĺĆexplicit confirmation„ÄĀauthorization„ÄĀauditšĽė„Āć„Āßwrite action„āíŤŅĹŚä†„Āô„āč„Äā
  • internal/admin endpoint„āídefault„ĀßŚÖ¨ťĖč„Āó„Ā™„ĀĄ„Äā
  • ťē∑śĖáprose„Āß„ĀĮ„Ā™„ĀŹstructured JSON result„āíŤŅĒ„Āô„Äā
  • tool execution error„Ā®protocol error„āíŚąÜ„ĀĎ„āč„Äābusiness/API validation failure„ĀĮ„ÄĀŚ£ä„āĆ„ĀüMCP session„Āß„ĀĮ„Ā™„ĀŹtool result„Āĺ„Āü„ĀĮtool execution error„Ā®„Āó„Ā¶ŤŅĒ„Āô„Äā
  • pagination„ÄĀfilter„ÄĀsummarizable field„Āßresult„āíbounded„ĀęšŅĚ„Ā§„Äā
  • prompt„ÄĀtool description„ÄĀresource content„ÄĀAPI output„āíprompt-injection surface„Ā®„Āó„Ā¶śČĪ„ĀÜ„Äā
  • stdio server„Āß„ĀĮstdout„āíMCP messageŚįāÁĒ®„Āę„Āô„āč„Äā
  • remote server„Āß„ĀĮHTTPS„ÄĀOAuth/token handling„ÄĀrate limit„ÄĀobservability„ÄĀkey rotation„ĀĮoptional extra„Āß„ĀĮ„Ā™„ĀŹserver„ĀģšłÄťÉ®„Äā

śóĘŚ≠ėAPI server„āíadapt„Āô„āčśé®Ś•®Ť®≠Ť®ą

śóĘŚ≠ėAPI server„Āß„ĀĮ„ÄĀrewrite„Āß„ĀĮ„Ā™„ĀŹadapter layer„Ā®„Āó„Ā¶Ť®≠Ť®ą„Āô„āč„Āģ„ĀĆśé®Ś•®„ÄāśóĘŚ≠ėAPI„āísource of truth„ĀęšŅĚ„Ā°„ÄĀOpenAPI„āícontract„Ā®„Āó„Ā¶šĹŅ„ĀĄ„ÄĀcurated„Āē„āĆ„ĀüMCP surface„Ā†„ĀĎ„āíŚÖ¨ťĖč„Āô„āč„Äā

śé®Ś•®layerśßčťÄ†

app/
  api/
    main.py              # Existing FastAPI app
    routers/
      inventory.py       # HTTP routes, response_model, operation_id, tags
  domain/
    inventory_service.py # Business logic shared by API and jobs
  mcp/
    server.py            # MCP adapter
    route_policy.py      # OpenAPI route filtering / mapping
    descriptions.py      # Tool/server description text
  tests/
    test_openapi_contract.py
    test_mcp_tools.py

śé®Ś•®dependency direction:

flowchart LR
    Domain["domain service"] --> API["FastAPI routes"]
    API --> OpenAPI["OpenAPI schema"]
    OpenAPI --> MCP["MCP adapter"]
    MCP --> Client["Claude / Codex / other MCP clients"]

# app/mcp/server.py
import httpx
from fastmcp import FastMCP
from app.api.main import app as fastapi_app
from app.config import settings
from app.mcp.route_policy import route_map_fn

openapi_spec = fastapi_app.openapi()

api_client = httpx.AsyncClient(
    base_url="http://127.0.0.1:9000",
    timeout=30.0,
    headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {settings.api_token}"},
)

mcp = FastMCP.from_openapi(
    openapi_spec=openapi_spec,
    client=api_client,
    name="Inventory MCP",
    route_map_fn=route_map_fn,
)

from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

router = APIRouter(prefix="/items", tags=["inventory"])

class ReserveRequest(BaseModel):
    quantity: int = Field(..., gt=0, description="Number of units to reserve.")

class ReserveResponse(BaseModel):
    item_id: str
    reserved: int
    remaining: int

@router.post(
    "/{item_id}/reserve",
    operation_id="reserve_inventory_item",
    summary="Reserve inventory for an item",
    description=(
        "Reserve stock for a known inventory item. "
        "This changes inventory state and should be called only after explicit user confirmation."
    ),
    response_model=ReserveResponse,
)
async def reserve_inventory_item(item_id: str, request: ReserveRequest) -> ReserveResponse:
    ...

śé®Ś•®route metadata:

routeŚÖ¨ťĖčpolicy

tag„Ā®path convention„āíšĹŅ„ĀĄ„ÄĀMCP exposure„āíreviewŚŹĮŤÉĹ„Āę„Āô„āč„Äā

# app/mcp/route_policy.py
from fastmcp.server.providers.openapi import MCPType
from fastmcp.utilities.openapi import HTTPRoute

BLOCKED_TAGS = {"internal", "admin", "debug"}
WRITE_METHODS = {"POST", "PUT", "PATCH", "DELETE"}

def route_map_fn(route: HTTPRoute, default_type: MCPType) -> MCPType | None:
    tags = set(route.tags or [])
    if tags.intersection(BLOCKED_TAGS):
        return MCPType.EXCLUDE
    if route.path.startswith(("/admin", "/debug", "/internal")):
        return MCPType.EXCLUDE
    if route.method in WRITE_METHODS:
        return MCPType.TOOL
    if route.method == "GET" and "catalog" in tags:
        return MCPType.RESOURCE_TEMPLATE
    return MCPType.TOOL

śé®Ś•®policy:

  • GET/search/list route„ĀĮclient support„ĀęŚŅú„Āė„Ā¶tool„Āĺ„Āü„ĀĮresource„Āę„Āß„Āć„āč„Äā
  • Write route„ĀĮśėéÁ§ļÁöĄ„Ā™action„Ā™„Āģ„Āßtool„Āģ„Āĺ„Āĺ„Āę„Āô„āč„Äā
  • Admin/debug/internal route„ĀĮ2śģĶťöé„Āßťô§Ś§Ė„Āô„āč„Äā„Āĺ„Āöinclude_in_schema=False„ĀßOpenAPI„Āč„āČťô§Ś§Ė„Āó„ÄĀś¨°„ĀęMCP route policy„Āßťô§Ś§Ė„Āô„āč„Äā
  • API„ĀĆŚ§ß„Āć„ĀĄ„ÄĀ„Āĺ„Āü„ĀĮsensitive„Ā™Ś†īŚźą„ÄĀproduction„Āß„ĀĮallowlist„Āč„āČŚßč„āĀ„āč„Äā

contract testšĺč:

def test_mcp_exposed_routes_have_ai_ready_metadata():
    spec = fastapi_app.openapi()
    for path, methods in spec["paths"].items():
        for method, operation in methods.items():
            if "internal" in operation.get("tags", []):
                continue
            assert operation.get("operationId")
            assert operation.get("summary")
            assert operation.get("description")
            assert operation.get("responses")

ProductionŤ¶ĀšĽ∂:

  • Private network„ÄĀVPN-only host„ÄĀfirewallŚÜÖ„Āģinternal service„ĀĮ„ÄĀAnthropic IP range„Āč„āČ„Āģaccess„āíŤ®ĪŚŹĮ„Āô„āč„Āč„ÄĀapproved gateway„āíšĹŅ„āŹ„Ā™„ĀĄťôź„āäŚčē„Āč„Ā™„ĀĄ„Äā

      "url": "${INVENTORY_MCP_URL:-https://mcp.example.com/mcp}",
      "oauth": {
        "scopes": "inventory:read inventory:reserve"
      },
      "timeout": 60000
    },
    "playwright": {
      "type": "stdio",
      "command": "npx",
      "args": ["-y", "@playwright/mcp@0.0.41"]
    }
  }
}

Protocol„ÄĀTransport„ÄĀAuth„ÄĀGovernance

śé•Á∂öprotocol / transport

MCP„Āę„ĀĮ1„Ā§„Āģprotocol message format„Ā®„ÄĀ„ĀĚ„Āģmessage„āíťĀč„Ā∂Ť§áśēį„ĀģśĖĻś≥ē„ĀĆ„Āā„āč„Äāmessage format„ĀĮJSON-RPC 2.0„Äātransport„ĀĮ„ÄĆclient„Ā®server„ĀĆJSON-RPC message„āíÁČ©ÁźÜÁöĄ„Āę„Ā©„ĀÜšļ§śŹõ„Āô„āč„Āč„Äć„ĀęÁ≠Ē„Āą„āč„āā„Āģ„Äā

ŚüļÁ§éÁźÜŤß£ŚźĎ„ĀĎ„ĀģśēīÁźÜ:

  • Protocol message: initialize„ÄĀtools/list„ÄĀtools/call„ÄĀresult„ÄĀerror„ÄĀnotification„Äā
  • Transport: stdio„ÄĀHTTP„ÄĀSSE stream„ÄĀ„ĀĚ„ĀģšĽĖbidirectional channel„Äā
  • Lifecycle: „Ā©„Āģtransport„Āß„āāŚźĆ„ĀėMCP lifecycle„ĀęŚĺď„ĀÜ„Äāinitialize -> initialized -> normal operation -> shutdown„Äā

ŚÖ®transportŚÖĪťÄö„Āģlifecycle

initialization phase„ĀĮoptional„Āß„ĀĮ„Ā™„ĀĄ„Äāclient„ĀĆinitialize„āíťĖčŚßč„Āó„ÄĀserver„ĀĆprotocol version„ÄĀcapability„ÄĀserver info„āíŤŅĒ„Āó„ÄĀ„ĀĚ„ĀģŚĺĆclient„ĀĆnotifications/initialized„āíťÄĀ„āč„Äā

sequenceDiagram
    participant C as MCP Client
    participant S as MCP Server
    C->>S: initialize(protocolVersion, clientCapabilities, clientInfo)
    S-->>C: InitializeResult(protocolVersion, serverCapabilities, serverInfo)
    C->>S: notifications/initialized
    C->>S: tools/list or resources/list
    S-->>C: available capabilities
    C->>S: tools/call
    S-->>C: tool result or error

OAuth/OIDC pattern

Pattern 1: machine-to-machine APIÔľąś©üśĘįťĖďAPIÔľČ

Agent -> Gateway -> target API
Gateway outbound auth: OAuth client credentials or IAM service role
Identity stores client secret / manages provider

ÁČĻŚģö„Āģhuman user„Āß„ĀĮ„Ā™„ĀŹ„ÄĀagent„ĀĆapplication„Ā®„Āó„Ā¶śĆĮ„āčŤąě„ĀÜŚ†īŚźą„ĀęšĹŅ„ĀÜ„Äā

Pattern 2: user-delegated SaaS„Āĺ„Āü„ĀĮMCP server

Agent user -> Gateway
Gateway target -> OAuth authorization code flow
Identity token vault stores user-scoped access/refresh token
Gateway calls target on behalf of that user

tool„ĀĆGitHub„ÄĀSlack„ÄĀGoogle„Ā™„Ā©user-scoped service„Āłaccess„Āô„āčŚŅÖŤ¶Ā„ĀĆ„Āā„āčŚ†īŚźą„ĀęšĹŅ„ĀÜ„Äā

Pattern 3: On-Behalf-Of / zero-trust downstreamÔľąšłčśĶĀzero-trustÔľČ

Inbound OIDC user token
  -> AgentCore Identity OBO token exchange
  -> downstream-scoped access token
  -> target API validates user + agent context

original user identity„āíšŅĚ„Ā°„Ā™„ĀĆ„āČ„ÄĀdownstream service„ĀĆGateway„Āß„ĀĮ„Ā™„ĀŹŤá™service„āíaudience„Ā®„Āô„āčtoken„āíŚŅÖŤ¶Ā„Ā®„Āô„āčŚ†īŚźą„ĀęšĹŅ„ĀÜ„Äā

Pattern 4: token passthroughÔľątoken„ĀģťÄöťĀéŤĽĘťÄĀÔľČ

Inbound token validated by Gateway authenticate-only
  -> same token forwarded to target
  -> target validates and authorizes

śÖéťáć„ĀęšĹŅ„ĀÜ„ÄāŚćėÁīĒ„Āß„ĀĮ„Āā„āč„ĀĆauthorization responsibility„āítarget„ĀłÁßĽ„Āó„ÄĀOBO token exchange„Ā®„ĀĮÁēį„Ā™„āč„Äā

śé®Ś•®AWS build pattern

Pattern A: śóĘŚ≠ėFastAPI/OpenAPI service

Ť®≠Ť®ąguidance:

  • targetŚÖ¨ťĖčŚČć„Āęadmin/debug/internal endpoint„āíťô§Ś§Ė„Āô„āč„Äā
  • user-scoped operation„Āß„ĀĮOAuth/OIDC„āíŚĄ™ŚÖą„Āô„āč„Äā

Pattern B: Lambda„Āę„āą„āčcustom internal tool

„ÄĆSkill = how to proceed / MCP = what to access or execute„Äć„Ā®„ĀĄ„ĀÜframe„ĀĮÁ∂≠śĆĀ„Āó„Ā§„Ā§„ÄĀoperation„ĀęŤźĹ„Ā®„Āô„ÄāPR repair„āĄdesign-to-code work„ĀĆśúČÁĒ®„Ā™šĺč„Āę„Ā™„āč„Äā
